MOSS-Audio-Thinking — Voice-Acting Caption Synthesis

Each clip is passed through the MOSS-Audio-Thinking reasoning models (4B & 8B, Qwen3 + a from-scratch 12.5 Hz audio encoder). The model listens to the audio itself and fuses three text aids: a Parakeet ASR transcript with per-sentence/word timestamps, a procedural whole-clip caption derived from expert VoiceNet / EmoNet / genuineness & vocal-burst classifiers, and the three LAION taxonomies (VoiceNet, EmoNet, VocalBurst).

It outputs the final voice-acting format: a GENERAL "how the whole voice sounds" instruction, then a SCRIPT where every sentence gets an inline (delivery cue), vocal (bursts) it actually hears, and [pause X.Xs] markers placed from the timestamps. The model may correct the ASR and relocate/insert bursts using its own listening.

ASR = Parakeet only (whisper-diarization omitted; VibeVoice/WaveVoice planned later). Greedy decoding. Progress: 4B 100/100 · 8B 100/100.
